class="x6smaf"><div class="dKWUte"><div data-hveid="CAYQDw"><span>November 04, 2017. Anyone planning a </span><b>Northern Lights</b><span> hunt in </span><b>Norway</b><span> needs to know their geography. This long, thin country's capital, Oslo, is too far south of the Arctic Circle to see the aurora borealis. So it's to </span><b>northern Norway</b><span> you should head, and Troms is firmly in the middle of the aurora zone.</span><a class="ZV5O1c"
